Free Hanfu cheongsam experience, you can take it back to your room and wear it as you like.

The most important thing is that a hotel is not as big as a large hotel, with limited guests and service staff. It is small, sophisticated and beautiful, so the service staff are very enthusiastic and very friendly.

Before I left, I took a baby with me and gave me a lot of suggestions for parent-child play, which was very considerate.

Just a few steps outside is Nanhu Tiandi, with beautiful night views and comprehensive dining and entertainment options. The house price of more than 500 yuan feels like a good value for money at this time.

posted:Posted February 1, 2024
msg:This is truly the most impressive hotel I've ever been to. First of all, the location is right in front of South Lake, and all the restaurants and cafes you can find in Shanghai are 5 minutes away. There is a small island called Hosimdeok in the center of Namho. It takes about 15 minutes to get on the boat, but the drop off point is only 1 minute from the hotel.

The hotel seems to have about 20 rooms on the second floor, and it feels like the staff remembers each and every guest. The rooms are great, the garden inside is really beautiful, and the hotel's restaurant also serves decent food at a reasonable price. The a**osphere is nice too.

It looks like there is something to see around South Lake, but I only went to Lake Lake because it was raining. I heard that this is a very meaningful place where Emperor Qianlong often stopped by during his tours and where various people gathered during the founding of China. So I felt very well managed and safe. The nearby water village is also good, but I recommend staying there for a day before going to Shanghai.

msg:I learned that the hotel is the base of the National Congress of the Communist Party of China in Jiaxing and a witness of the National Congress of the Communist Party of China. I was very excited to book it.
The hotel is very easy to find. The location is particularly good. It is located in the scenic spot. On the edge is the South Lake and the tourist information center. Even if you are visiting temporarily, you can easily obtain the scenic spot information (such as: where is the pier where you can take the boat, etc.)
From the restaurant, you can see the scenery of South Lake, and you can walk a few steps out of the hotel to come to the shore and look at the red boat in the distance.
The breakfast is very rich, injecting enough energy to start the whole day of travel. The small garden in the hotel has a unique feeling. There is also a guzheng in it. It is very comfortable and relaxing to sit in it when you are tired from playing.
In addition to the convenience, the hotel's facilities are also very good, and the rest is very comfortable. I will choose to stay here next time
